<h1 class="entry-title">Yahoo! calls Kenya “country of Obama’s birth”</h1>
<div class="td-module-meta-info">
<div class="td-post-author-name"><div class="td-author-by">By</div> <a href="https://www.dcclothesline.com/author/dr-eowyn/">Dr. Eowyn</a><div class="td-author-line"> - </div> </div> <span class="td-post-date"><time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2013-06-23T14:15:15+00:00">June 23, 2013</time></span> </div>
</header>
</div>
</div>

<p>Last Friday, June 21, 2013, in an article about the POS’s trip to Africa, Rachel Rose Hartman of Yahoo! News called Kenya “the country of his birth”!<span id="more-10977"></span></p>
<p>Someone at Yahoo! caught the Freudian slip of truth, and the reference to Obama being born in Kenya was deleted from a later version of the article.</p>
<p>Alas for Yahoo!, by then a screenshot of the original article already had been captured — for posterity. LOL</p><div class="code-block code-block-8" style="margin: 8px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;">
<div class="ads_container" website_id="2060" widget_id="5626"></div><script async="" src="https://cdn.whizzco.com/scripts/widget/widget_v3.js" type="text/javascript"></script>
</div>

<p>Noel Sheppard reports for <a href="http://newsbusters.org/blogs/noel-sheppard/2013/06/22/birther-update-yahoo-news-says-obama-was-born-kenya" target="_blank">Newsbusters</a>, June 22, 2013:</p>
<p>It appears someone at Yahoo! News has opened one too many email messages from Orly Taitz.</p><div class="code-block code-block-7" style="margin: 8px 0; clear: both;">
<h3 class="title">Trending:</h3>
<ul class="wpp-list">
<li> <a class="wpp-post-title" href="https://www.dcclothesline.com/2023/03/02/tainted-blood-80-of-the-blood-supply-contaminated-with-spike-proteins-from-mrna-jabs-blood-banks-accidentally-admit/" target="_self">TAINTED BLOOD: 80% of the blood supply contaminated with spike proteins from mRNA jabs, blood banks accidentally admit</a> <span class="wpp-meta post-stats"><span class="wpp-views">1.4k views</span></span></li>
</ul>
</div>
<p>On Friday, the website actually published a piece claiming Kenya was Barack Obama’s country of birth: […]</p>
<div>
<p>Someone eventually caught the error as there is <a href="http://news.yahoo.com/blogs/ticket/obama-administration-defers-security-africa-trip-costs-skips-211646601.html">now a correction</a>:</p>
<blockquote><p><em>Correction: An earlier version of this story incorrectly identified the president’s birthplace.</em></p>
<p>President Barack Obama makes the first extended trip to Africa of his presidency next week—but he won’t be stopping in his ancestral homeland.</p></blockquote>
<p>H/t <a href="http://www.examiner.com/article/yahoo-news-says-obama-born-kenya-edits-article" target="_blank">Examine</a>r and Dean of <a href="https://www.dcclothesline.com/" title="New blog by a great conservative patriot">The D. C. Clothesline</a>.</p>
